Slowly, still breathing me in, he drags his nose along the length of mine. <br><br>“You tie me up in knots.” He presses my mouth with his. Briefly. Then he withdraws, breathing hard, and looks at me with heavy-lidded eyes. “I want to play you a thousand different songs so you get a clue of what … I feel inside me…”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>I also completely adored Brooke. She’s had her hopes and dreams shattered at a young age and is now trying to carve out a new path for herself. She’s a tower of strength to Remy, represents everything he thinks he is not good enough for but she is, beyond a shadow of a doubt, falling irrevocably in love with Remy but she doesn’t understand what he is hiding from her and why is he is holding back. When she does eventually discover his secret, she chose to stand by her man through thick and thin whatever the future may bring and I loved her for it. Remy may be the epitome of a hard, tough masculine physique but the emotional strength and fortitude lies with Brooke. Remy needs her and will never be able to let her go.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I’m so fucking in love with you I don’t even know what to do with myself anymore.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>As Remy continues to hold back and Brooke practically melts with desire and unsatisfied arousal, the sexual tension between the two of them built to such an incredible intensity that I was so unbelievably turned on and desperate for them to make good on all this pent up emotion. The sex is very hot and the scenes beautifully erotic but what makes this extra special is the emotion in those scenes is powerfully palpable and leaps right off the page. You know just how much this means to them and, now that they’re together, I began to fear what was ahead and what was likely to tear them apart and I couldn’t bear the thought of that – I knew how much it would hurt Remy and I cared so much about him by this time and my heart was breaking for him.<br><br>As the events of the final few chapters unfolded and I realised what Remy had done and why, my eyes once again started to fill with tears and by the time we got to the last few pages, I was all out sobbing, ugly crying. A book hasn’t made me cry like that in ages – it’s so incredibly emotional, so soulful, so heartfelt. The writing is sublime – I was right there with the characters in every single scene, I could see everything, especially the pulsating energy of the fight scenes and the raucous crowds. Most of all I could see Remy – he lived vividly in my imagination, he was REAL to me. There’s a scene when Brooke climbs into the shower with him and, of all the scenes in the book, this one lived the most vividly in my imagination – not really sure why but it seemed so incredibly intense and emotional.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I open the glass shower door, and step inside with his beautiful slick skin and big hard muscles, pressing my naked breasts to his back as I wrap my arms around his waist. He groans and tugs my arms tighter around him, and the words I love you are there inside me. I've never loved anyone in my life and I never imagined it could be like this.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is just about the perfect book for me – it has just exact right mix of eroticism and emotion and it’s beautifully paced. I loved the way Remy’s eyes would slide to Brooke just before a fight, the way he would stare at her trying to read her, the way they shared songs to say what they could not put into words – I loved everything. The anticipation of them finally getting together was frying my brain and I could not put this book down and I read deep into the wee small hours to finish it with a pair of headphones on and sobbing away! It’s beautiful, soulful, compelling, powerful and quite simply just exquisite.<br><br>As I look back on my reading experience with this book and think about how it made me feel, I know that I have been in the presence of greatness.<br><br><b>There’s now a piece of my heart that will forever belong to Remington ‘Riptide’ Tate. </b> <br><br>5 incredible stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418898i/829871._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo remywhisperingtobrooke_zps34ffac76.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13876752716172627857">I JUST CAN'T GET OVER THIS BOOK. I JUST CAN'T.<br/><br/>1 heart clenching star...to this heart clenching romance...clenching clenching clenching like nothing ever clenched before.<br/><br/>This book was about a girl named Brooke who obviously has some sort of clenching condition.   <span id="freeText13876752716172627857" style="display:none">I JUST CAN'T GET OVER THIS BOOK. I JUST CAN'T.<br /><br />1 heart clenching star...to this heart clenching romance...clenching clenching clenching like nothing ever clenched before.<br /><br />This book was about a girl named Brooke who obviously has some sort of clenching condition. I can't count the times or list parts of her that clenched in many, <i>many</i> ways.<br /><br />Every time Remy was near she was panting like a dog in heat and I just wanted to pull her out of my Kindle and hit her. And hit her. Again and again.<br /><br />Look. I totally got that she thought he was so hot she was burning up with clenching and needing and what the eff ever it was.<br /><br />But seriously. She's at it for 80% of this book. At one point, I was one-hundred-and-one percent sure that the author was making a joke out of it.<br /><br />Not only does she clench at the sight of him, at touching him, at whatevering him, but she actually clenches at remembering the sight of him, touching him, whatevering him. I kept waiting for her to clench at remembering clenching at remembering the sight of him, touching him, whatevering him. Et cetera, et cetera.<br /><br />By the end I was almost positive that she actually did have a clenching condition. Her core/muscles/p**sy clenches a lot, but so do her hands, fingers, toes, heart - you name it, it probably clenched in this book.<br />I kept imagining her spasming because she was clenching so much.<br />Please note that her muscles/core/p**sy/pit of her stomach also: tingles, tightens, warms. But mostly she clenches.<br /><br />And not only that - but it's contagious because, yeah, you got it right, Remy clenches and so do his friends, and I think I really lost count of all the people that clench in this book.<br /><br />Oh, and there's also this sweet subplot love story with crazy chemistry between Ms. Clench and Remy.<br /><br />The word clench, people, is used seventy times throughout the book in all its forms. I see a red flag go up. HOW did nobody catch this.<br /><br />I do wish the author didn't force her tastes on me while reading the book, though. I like Goo Goo Dolls, but I don't think I'll ever listen to Iris again.<br />She also sort of explains to you what VERY popular songs and movies are about. Make of that what you will.<br /><br />There are a couple of graphic sex scenes.<br /><br />Overall? I wouldn't <i>not</i> recommend this book. I wouldn't recommend it either. I'd just sort of shrug. I didn't care for it even if it did have some very sweet/intense/funny/amazing moments.<br /><br />edit: I originally gave this book 2 stars. I've just changed my mind.<br />I didn't want to talk about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Remy's manic depression <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> in my review, and I still don't want to, but having personal experience with that I thought it was dealt with in a very irresponsible manner and frankly, I felt slightly insulted at some things that went on/were said.<br />But that's all I'm saying.<br /><br />edit2: I just couldn't leave it be. I feel like I owe it to the author to say what exactly I didn't like about this book (other than the fact it had me <i>clenching</i> my teeth). It really wasn't my intention to trash the book, and I don't wanna come off as a reviewer that just hated on it for the sake of hating. I didn't hate this book, I just didn't love it either.<br /><br />ONE<br />There are numerous fighter books that are all a variation of a theme, and this one finally, FINALLY, had potential to be something more. There is nothing worse than wasted potential.<br />I can definitely see the allure of smut without substance (who am I kidding? I can't, not really), but it could have been so much deeper than it was.<br />Instead of reading a book about Remy and Brooke healing each other and being what the other needs, it was trivialized by turning this into a juvenile "why won't he eff me? he's so hot. ovaries explode." book.<br />It's not really all the clenching, that was me actually trying to find some humor in reading this book, otherwise I wouldn't have gone through it all the way.<br /><br />TWO<br />The writing is amateurish at best. Written in first person POV present tense - which I can tolerate, but it keeps switching tenses throughout. Please, no. It's an aneurysm waiting to happen.<br />Someone obviously proof-read this as it was really low on typos, considering, and I'd even say it was a fairly well edited book.<br />But there were sentences that made no sense. There were misused words. It was repetitive.<br />I admire the author's efforts because I really thought she might have had a good story here if it weren't for the fact that being in Brooke's head was worse than being in Bella Swan's head and I hated, hated Bella.<br />The heroine overshares to the point of being disgusting. Her ovaries cramp, her womb clenches, her nipples harden and it's a constant state of unbearable arousal that is so unrealistic I had to fight not to roll my eyes every time she would say anything about it.<br /><br />She literally views Remy as a piece of meat, he's all man, he's huge, his muscles this, his jaw that, his spiky hair, his this, his that, oh, the obligatory pants (jeans, whatever) that hang on his hips...she wants to lick him, to jump him, to I-don't-even-know...<br />It's objectifying and superficial at its worst. Not to mention swamped with cliches.<br />By the time she started showing Brooke maybe falling for Remy's personality it was already too late for me.<br /><br />I still believe Remy was the highlight of this book. That's a good character, if only she gave him a touch more personality. I'm not the one to go for silent and broody, but I can see why it's attractive, however, Remy just grunts and groans and grumbles and growles throughout this book. Just when I was okay and accepted the fact that he's simply not a man of many words, he spills his heart out in a long-winded speech that is basically a recap of the book in his POV.<br /><br />The ending was rushed and a bit of a "it was all a dream" solution. "Hey, it was just a big misunderstanding. We cool now?"<br /><br />THREE<br />The author obviously did her research. I was kind of bored with all the muscle names and nutritional information, but I loved the fighting aspect of the story. I would have enjoyed it so much more if it weren't for the cop-out in the end.<br /><br />BUT. But, the depiction of Remy's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[bipolar disorder <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was mostly off mark.<br /><br />And I beg you, authors, don't use mental disorders and illnesses, rape and near rape, eating disorders, domestic abuse (NOT all of these are in this book, this is more of a general thing) or anything similar just as a plot device.<br />Moreover, don't be irresponsible about using these sensitive subjects. Suggesting that mood-stabilizers and anti-depressants are no good is not a responsible action. You hold the power of a written word in your hands that, maybe, hundreds, thousands will read. Please don't suggest people they are better off not medicating something as serious as Remy's condition.<br />Remy is sedated by Pete and Riley on a regular basis and I just don't know how that is more okay than just seeking proper kind of help. They bring him hookers while he's out of it and it seriously rubbed me the wrong way.<br /><br />Okay, now I've calmed down from the high that was this book, I guess my thoughts sound a lot more coherent. I hate writing negative reviews without actually adding something substantial to them.<br /><br />edit3 lmao:<br />And for the love of everything you cherish, if anyone wants to comment with a "don't take it so seriously, it's just a book", just please refrain from doing it. When I want to read a book that is not serious, I read a comedy.<br /><br />edit4: I JUST CAN'T LEAVE IT BE.<br />After giving it A LOT of thought (I literally can't stop thinking about it), today I've decided the book pissed me off.<br />How irresponsible do you have to be to write something like this?!<br /><br />Relying on tranquilizers to control his behavior when he's having an episode is probably the most irresponsible thing I have ever heard.<br /><br />I really hope the author will get Remy some proper, medical help in the next book.<br /><br />Having <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[bipolar disorder <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> DOES NOT mean you end up in a looney bin. They were freaking treating him like he's crazy when this illness is treated like any other illness today. I just can't fathom this.<br />It is so obvious it was in there just for drama's sake.<br /><br />I live in a freaking stone age country compared to the States and even here people are treated for what they have, and not kept in a psych ward just because they're depressed unless they're a threat to themselves (which, let's be honest, Remy maybe even was).<br /><br />GOD. I just can't get over this whole thing.<br /><br />I make it a point to stay away from books about these heavy issues because of all the REAL books out there that treat these things with so little respect it makes me want to gag.<br /><br />If I could unread a book, I'd choose REAL, just to keep my sanity. And I have read some pretty horrible books.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer568870422" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17849928047582975851"><b>Don't be fooled by all the 5 star reviews on this book!</b><br/><br/> I'm sure there's an okay story in there somewhere if you don't have any problem with digging through a bunch of nonsensical crap to find it. I don't want to spend my time trying to figure out what the author means, I just want to get lost in the story and characters. <br/><br/>For me this book was close to unreadable. It is riddled with bad grammar, long run-on sentences (some entire paragraphs are one long sentence) misused words galore, incorrect t</span>
  <span id="freeText17849928047582975851" style="display:none"><b>Don't be fooled by all the 5 star reviews on this book!</b><br /><br /> I'm sure there's an okay story in there somewhere if you don't have any problem with digging through a bunch of nonsensical crap to find it. I don't want to spend my time trying to figure out what the author means, I just want to get lost in the story and characters. <br /><br />For me this book was close to unreadable. It is riddled with bad grammar, long run-on sentences (some entire paragraphs are one long sentence) misused words galore, incorrect tenses, improper sentence structure and most of the sentences make little to no sense at all even if you rearranged them. It was poorly written with almost no character development and the h's inner monologue is juvenile and extremely repetitive and drags on for pages at a time.<br /><br />Some examples. <br /><br /><i>"Because your smile doesn't even have any place on your face anymore."</i> What?<br /><br /><i>"I spent extra time rubbing his deltoids, the roundest, squarest part of the shoulder."</i> Roundest and squarest? Hmmm.<br /><br /><i>"We need to stop, sometimes we hear music, turn on the TV, or eat."</i> Uh, I think she meant listen not hear.<br /><br /><i>"He buzzes his nose into my temple."</i> I don't even know.<br /><br /><i>"and now he's just bouncing on his calves as if waiting for the next hit to come."</i> He's got mad skills cause that seems impossible. <br /><br /><i>"Its hard to watch you fight but to watch you suicide yourself is..."</i> Really? REALLY?<br /><br /><i>"She shoots some sort of tranquilizer up his IUV."</i> It's just an IV. No U needed.<br /><br /><i>"That my floor was shaking under my feet. It was."</i> Was there an earthquake?<br /><br /><i>"I'd do it a thousand times for you." He scents me. And I scent him."</i> You mean smells, I'm pretty sure. Or else they're peeing on each other?<br /><br />These are not single instances. They run rampant through the entire book and the same mistakes are made often, sometimes several on a single page, so it obviously wasn't an editing or typo issue. Just the authors lack of knowledge. The sex scenes had this same issue with wording that caused them to just be ridiculous. "Breast tips" Are you for real with this? Now this one's just personal but calling the bad guys "goonies". It's just goons. Every time she said that all I could think of was Sloth with Chunk and little Data standing behind him throwing gang symbols and trying to look tough. Goonies never say die! Not so intimidating. <br /><br />I'm not even going to go into what little storyline there was. It's pretty much just the h's immature lusting over the H's muscles and jawline and sweatpants hanging off his hips just so, repeated over and over and over. She actually gushes a few times when he sips off her drink because their lips touched the same thing. *facepalm* Not much depth with any other character in the story either. Most of it was unbelievably boring. I will say there were some aspects i.e the song sharing &amp; the H's illness, that had the story been better executed could've made for some great reading. But that didn't happen. The way the mental illness was handled was particularly off putting. He shouldn't put that poison in his body. She says. i.e medication. Again, for real? <br /><br />Bottom line is, if you actually care about a story being well written and not just a bunch of barely legible nonsense with a semi-hot guy that hardly talks and an immature rambling heroine, then you should pass on this one. Honestly, I wish I had. <br /><br />eta: to match Ammy review.</span>

<div id="review_561690152" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561690152" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561690152?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561690152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15787462984502468385"><b>Jenny:</b> We can never get enough of MMA book with a tortured hero can we Gitte? But what I found with this one was that there was a twist with regard to the MC which I found quite different and, as sad as that was, I enjoyed that this delved a little further than being a romance. Remy was at the heart of this story and I found him such troubled and interesting character.<br/><br/><i>A fallen boxer.<br/>A woman with a broken dream.<br/>A competition…</i><br/><br/>Remington Tate. Remy. Riptide. We know him by many names, but knowing th</span>
  <span id="freeText15787462984502468385" style="display:none"><b>Jenny:</b> We can never get enough of MMA book with a tortured hero can we Gitte? But what I found with this one was that there was a twist with regard to the MC which I found quite different and, as sad as that was, I enjoyed that this delved a little further than being a romance. Remy was at the heart of this story and I found him such troubled and interesting character.<br /><br /><i>A fallen boxer.<br />A woman with a broken dream.<br />A competition…</i><br /><br />Remington Tate. Remy. Riptide. We know him by many names, but knowing the man. What makes him tick, what drives Remy’s compulsive and at times unpredictable behaviour? Where does his anger, confusion and uncertainty stem from? Why was he so tortured and could Brooke be his salvation? Was she going to be the woman who sees so much more than the angry, manic fighter the fans see? That’s what I wanted to unravel and I couldn’t wait to find out.<br /><br />Remy finds it hard to communicate, finding it hard to express himself and is most definitely a man of few words, and this again was something I really wanted to further explore.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Your name,” he growls, panting, his eyes wild on mine.<br />“It’s Brooke Dumas,” she says, and then she happily shoots out my cell phone number. To my chagrin.<br />His lips curl and he meets my gaze. “Brooke Dumas.” He just fucked my name right in front of me.</i>
</b><br /><br />Brooke knocks Remy for a six when he first locks eyes with her and continues to be confused by the intense feelings he has for her. Unable to precisely communicate his emotions through thought and words, Remy uses music/songs to express his feelings and this was such a poignant and beautiful part of the story and being an absolute music nut, I LOVED it!<br />The author put a lot of effort into having the right songs for Remy and Brooke, even so far as to obtaining lyrics, and I’m so glad she did because this really did add to the story. I know there is one song in particular I will listen to from now on and always think of Brooke and Remy. Somehow the author turned it into “their song” for me and I loved that.<br /><br /><b>Gitte:</b> I loved this story Jenny, for so many reasons, not just for the obvious ones like the fact that we have a gorgeous tortured hero in Remy, but the fact that this one absolutely put a different spin to the typical MMA stories out there. Remy is a complete force of nature. He is F.I.E.R.C.E! Like the dangerous quiet before the devastating storm. There is something so utterly raw and intense about Remy that just traps the reader…he exudes this power that is unrivalled. He makes you miss a breath. He is like no other. He left me speechless!<br /><br />What I loved most about him though is the way he communicates through music. Remy is a man after my own heart. He reduced me to a puddle on the floor by his feet in complete captivation and desire.<br /><br />His immediate and intense attraction to Brooke, an attraction he is unable to communicate, gave me chills.<br /><br />You cannot relax into this story completely as the danger is there and you just don’t know which way it’s going to go. Remy was complex and his story broke my heart…made me cry! This Author had me gripped and on the edge of my seat through the whole story, oh and the music…spot on!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>He steps forward, and his damp hand slides into the nape of my neck. My pulse skitters as he lowers his dark head to set a small, dry kiss on my lips. It feels like he’s marking me. Like he’s preparing me for something monumental. That could both change and ruin my life.</i>
</b> <br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> You’re so right Gitte. In a way, you do read this with some measure of dread in your heart because you feel so much for this tormented man. Brooke is a tough cookie and tries to deny her feelings for the intensely closed off Remy, who fights as a way of dealing with his aggression. This man brings out such a need in Brooke she is unsure of how to proceed with Remy but knows she has to proceed with caution.<br /><br />As her physio it is her job to keep this man in peak condition, to make him ready for every fight on his calender, to take care of him and keep him in peak condition physically and mentally.<br /><br />Remy relies on Brooke in more ways than one and his feelings are so extreme towards her she must be guard herself against the intense and unpredictable Remy. Remy, what can I say about Remy? Loved him. Remy will melt your heart. He will break your heart at times and you will want to just grab this big bear of a man and hold him. Hold him until you make everything right for Remy. His has not been an easy road. <br /><br />Misjudged, used and misunderstood, but with Brooke by his side, can she help him tame his demons and be the Remy he desperately wants to be? I really enjoyed Real, it was a different take on a theme I love, the sexual chemistry was off the charts and I’m so glad I got to read Brooke and Remy’s story. A story with heart about a man who will steal it. The ending completely melted me.<br /><br /><b>Gitte:</b> Brooke was a great heroine. She too has had emotional trauma in her past and it has shaped her into who she is the day she meets Remy and affects her actions from then on in respect to the intensity of feelings she has for him. Brooke has had to change her life and find her place and now has the added uncertainty of Remy.<br /><br />Remy has so much turmoil within him yet lacks the words. The reasons for who Remy is, his struggles and his aggression he cannot put into words. By keeping Brooke at his side he tries to show her, tries to convey who he really is through music, show her another side. Brooke reciprocates and I thought this journey was absolutely beautiful and breathtaking at times despite the ugly and gritty rearing its head throughout. <br />The sexual tension was so intense, built up to the extreme so that you literally can’t take any more.<br /><br />I loved this story and without a doubt I absolutely fell in total LOVE with Remy. I applaud this new Author for taking a different path in the genre of MMA romance. It worked and she nailed it!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Brooke,” he growls softly, meaningfully, against my lips, as he draws back with a smile. “I’m Remington.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>ARC supplied by author for an honest review</i><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15787462984502468385" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3767802827989288323" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>3.5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: Contemporary Romance<br>Review Posted on 4/17/13<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413916ra/815527.gif" alt=" photo ad-tomato-throw_zps9bf1dc27.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, so before you throw tomatos at me in protest just hear me out.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413916i/815528.jpg" alt=" photo 17617277_zpsb3dfdaea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413916i/815529.jpg" alt=" photo 38663fca6aa874f1184eb9fe6a0be9ac_zps28b6f1e6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Remington RIPTIDE Tate is #1 in the underground fighting circuit girls wanna scew him and guys want to be him. Brooke allowed her best friend, Melanie, to talk her in to going to the underground matches. As Melanie screeches her love for RIPTIDE, Brooke can’t help but be pulled into his magnetic force field of high electric energy. And she also can’t stop the fact that after one look from Remy she now desires him just like every other woman in the building. Of course she chooses that moment to flee.<br><br>After making quick work of his opponent Remy goes after Brooke. Melanie overhears the introductions and gives Remy Brooke’s number. Much to Brooke’s dismay. Dismayed no more, Brooke is unemployed at the moment and Remy not only offers her tickets for his next match he also follows it up with a job offer. She accepts.<br> <br>She wants him and he wants her but before he has her, he must tell her the truth.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413916i/815530._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 09036d71-9e01-476b-b600-ddb2a2505b79_zps688a09c8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Can Brooke accept the <i>REAL</i> man who is Remington RIPTIDE Tate?</b><br><br><br><br>First let me be clear I did like this book, I will not sit here and act like Katy Evans did not get my panties all in a twist over Remy because she did. Had my ass wanting to hump something like a damn dog in heat.. No lie.LOL!! Remy put out some good swoon worthy vibes. I mean HELLO how can you not when she writes things like<br><br><i>'My legs wobble, and I’m left with the distinct impression this man wants to pound me next. With his cock.'</i> ~Brooke<br><br><i>'He suckles, sucks, turns, twists. I fall in love with his kiss so fast, that soon I don’t know where my hands are, where I’m lying. My entire body is consumed by the way he fucks my mouth until my lips are raw and swollen and it hurts to kiss him back even though my frenzied body demands more.'</i> ~Brooke<br><br>And then words like <b>
  <u>mind-blowing pleasure bolts</u>
</b><br><br><i>My arms clench around his strong neck as he teases the very tip of his finger inside, and a <b>mind-blowing pleasure bolts</b> through me.</i> ~Brooke<br><br>I mean<b> COME ON</b> we all want to be <i>sucked-fucked-plucked-twisted- bound-gagged and pounded</i> into, right?!! Oh..wait may be that last bit is just me*shrugs shoulders* <b>WHATEVER</b> you get my drift! *wink,wink*<br><br><br><b>I’ll start with what I did like</b><br>The anticipation and build up to Brooke and Remy having sex had me horny as shit. <i>I'm talking jump your man as soon as he walks in the door, HORNY.</i> Now not everyone is a fan of the clenching uterus… Well it bothered me none. I was in deep <i>deep</i> anticipation and was pretty much panting until they sealed the deal. I think Evans did a good job of building up that climax and hit it out the park once the deed was done. <br>– I also enjoyed Remy and his alpha glory <br>– I adored the scenes where they swapped iPod's and played each other music that was so damn cute!!! <br>– I agreed with his decision to wait until after Brooke knew about his…condition for sex <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ He is Bipolar <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>- My fave scene was the one with the roses. No denying that was pretty H O T and there was nothing sexual about it. <br><br><b>What I did not like so much was</b><br>- Brooke and all her damn muscle terminology<br>- Brooke and her stupid brain fart moment with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Scorpio.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>– Brooke's lusting became a bit repetitive along with her internal monologues. I am BIG on character interaction and this chick was in her head a bit much for my taste buds. It just made me want more Remy.<br>- Remy going from 0 to 60 in a millisecond was crazy and may be accurate.. but what’s the deal with him not remembering things… Is that accurate?? I need to look that up(thinks to self..)<br>- The entire plot with Brooke’s sister Nora fell flat for me. If anything I wanted to see Remy KICK DAT ASS. The whole Scorpio setup was to predictable. I don’t mind predictable but like I said it just fell flat for me. <br><br>OVERALL -I’m clearly in a very small minority here…so here is the deal, while I may have enjoyed REAL and all that is Remington RIPTIDE the fact of the matter is the story did not move me.<u> And that is why I gave it 3 STARS.</u> Believe me I love an alpha male just as much as the next girl,however I just found that the story itself did not take me to that place of being forever etched in to my brain. But whatever, it seemed to do that for mostly everyone else. Surprisingly, or maybe not so surprisingly, I loved Remy yet did not connect with Brooke. Go figure.<br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Loved Remy<br>Writing Style- Good, I actually like Katy Evan's style it was the story that I was not overly excited about.<br>Plot/Storyline- Fair<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I liked it, I just did not love it!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

And her little sister was always the one who was interested in boys growing up, while Brooke would rather have an Olympic gold medal.<br><br>Brooke has never looked at those with the ‘y’ chromosome as anything other than silly boys.<br><br>Which is why when her best friend drags her along to an underground fighting match, her world is ROCKED by a <i>man</i> with fighting gloves on his hands and sex on his smile.<br><br><b>
  <i> I want to go crazy. Bungee. Sprint again, even if only in a literal sense. All those dates I never had, because I was training for something that never happened. Never drinking. Keeping my grades up so I could do track. Remington Tate is everything I’ve never, ever done, and I have a condom tucked in my bag and suddenly I know exactly why I put it there. This guy is a fighter. I want to touch his beautiful chest and I want to kiss those lips. I want to have those hands on me.” </i>
</b><br><br>Brooke is the beauty, and Remington is the beast in this wildfire of a book.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_li49zf8UgI1qcsui0o1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>But like every beast, he has his secrets.<br><br>Secrets that can push even a strong young woman like Brooke away.<br><br>And Remington ‘Riptide’ Tate will go toe-to-toe with the devil in himself to ensure that doesn’t happen.<br><br><b>
  <i>You can’t, Brooke. You can’t leave.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/sex-sex-and-sexuality-32551601-348-500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> You’re mine. </i>
</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11795924185797342158">NOW LIVE ON AMAZON!!<br/><br/>KINDLE LINK:<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Real-ebook/dp/B00C9QORFW/ref=tmm_kin_title_0'>http://www.amazon.com/Real-ebook/dp/B...</a><br/><br/>PAPERBACK LINK:<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Real-Katy-Evans/dp/1482335395/ref=tmm_pap_title_0'>http://www.amazon.com/Real-Katy-Evans...</a><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>GENRE</b>: Categorized as NA, but, honestly, it's adult contemporary. There will be a follow-up book</span>
  <span id="freeText11795924185797342158" style="display:none">NOW LIVE ON AMAZON!!<br /><br />KINDLE LINK:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Real-ebook/dp/B00C9QORFW/ref=tmm_kin_title_0">http://www.amazon.com/Real-ebook/dp/B...</a><br /><br />PAPERBACK LINK:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Real-Katy-Evans/dp/1482335395/ref=tmm_pap_title_0">http://www.amazon.com/Real-Katy-Evans...</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>GENRE</b>: Categorized as NA, but, honestly, it's adult contemporary. Both characters are in their early-mid twenties and have careers. 18+<br /><br /><b>HEAT LEVEL</b>: I'm pretty sure it cannot be adequately rated! See my review.<br /><br /><b>*New* INTENSITY LEVEL</b>: Un. Be. Lievable. See my review.<br /><br /><b>NOTE</b>: Book #1 of The Real, Raw &amp; Ripped Series, <b>BUT</b> this is a complete story!!! There will be a follow-up book from Remy's POV, as well as a third book. However, this story is whole, and there are <b>NO CLIFFHANGERS!!</b><br /><br /><br /><b>5 REAL Stars!!</b><br />My prediction? REAL is <b>The Next Big Thing</b>, and Katy Evans is <i>going places</i>! HolyfreakingOMG, people!! I have never, <i>not ever</i>, read the kind of insane chemistry and level of intensity that is in this book! I have a new obsession, and his name? The two words you wanna remember? <i>REMINGTON TATE</i>. <br /><br />Remington Tate is THE star of the scary-dangerous underground fighting circuit. Once a former pro boxer, he fell from grace and has made a new name for himself in the underground. Brooke Dumas had been so close to living her dream she could smell, taste and touch it. But, all of that died with one serious injury. Now she's been hired as Remington Tate's sports rehab specialist. Brooke knows exactly what she wants from him. She simply cannot help herself because he attracts her mind and body in ways that she has no ability to fight. Remy is the single most compelling and confusing man she has ever encountered. There is something very different about him, and it drags her along in his wake. He often 'speaks' to Brooke in the choice of song he plays for her. She knows they have a connection unlike any she knew existed. But...what does he actually want from her and, more importantly, can she survive it?<br /><br /><b>WOW x 100</b> would not be an understatement when it comes to REAL. I don't even know where to start or how to properly do it justice in a review. <br /><br />Until you have read and experienced the chemistry, the intensity, the heat...there is simply no way for me to even get close to adequately expressing what this story, this relationship, these characters...REMINGTON will do to you as a woman. My mind and body were <i>buzzing</i> while reading this book, and I've been feeling the aftershocks for several days now! I'm almost positive that my ebook was releasing pheromones! I LIVE for stories with fantastic chemistry and high intensity, and REAL was, OMG, both!!<br /><br />REAL is written with a kind of rough and raw prose and style, and this is something else I absolutely adore, particularly for this story. It would not have worked any other way. Katy Evans (and all who collaborated to bring this book to life), amazing job. Amazing!<br /><br />The characters? What can I say? I loved them ALL. The focus is absolutely on Remy and Brooke in this story, but the secondary characters do add something essential. Brooke...that girl reeled me in. I wasn't certain how I felt about her in the very early part of the book, but, once you get past the first chapter (<i>and that's important...get past the first chapter and get into the meat of the story</i>), I fell in love with her. She knows her job, and Katy Evans did an amazing job with Brooke's internal dialogue. I loved how she expressed her attraction to Remy, especially, in such a fascinatingly semi-scientific way. I know, I know. But, trust me. It makes her so authentic....and, strangely, it's hot ;-)<br /><br />Then we get to Remington. Good. God. Almighty. I am thoroughly OBSESSED! What a complex individual. What a fighter. What a tease. What a sexual being. What a...<b>MAN</b>! He absolutely broke my heart, and he <i>spoke</i> to me. I got him. I really did. I hope everyone else will, as well. He is damaged, and he is dealing with a truly serious issue. Truly serious. He's also insanely raw and primal! He's obviously Alpha, but it's tempered with a resigned sadness and vulnerability that makes him unlike any Alpha I've read before. He's the most real Alpha I've ever read before. He <i>is</i>...REAL.<br /><br />Please, whatever you do, give REAL a chance to work its magic and pheromones on you;) Honestly, I don't think I have to worry. This book is one you're going to hear A LOT about. Katy Evans? Girl, congrats. You know I'm waiting for my next Remy fix! You rocked this one <b>HARD</b>.<br /><br /><br />**ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**</span>
  <a data-text-id="11795924185797342158" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2404321085" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12309928239210634299"><b>This book is oozing testosterone...</b><br/>All this sniffing, rubbing, growling and mating hormones...<br/>hahaha<br/><br/>I loved it!<br/><br/>I was thinking of writing a detailed review, but then I had a look at all these 1-star reviews and I honestly laughed my socks off. Almost all of them are brilliant! Better than all the 5-stars reviews actually.<br/><br/>On the other hand, I am wondering what people expect to read when they start a story about an oversexed underground fighter and a sweet ex-athlete who doesn't understand what thi</span>
  <span id="freeText12309928239210634299" style="display:none"><b>This book is oozing testosterone...</b><br />All this sniffing, rubbing, growling and mating hormones...<br />hahaha<br /><br />I loved it!<br /><br />I was thinking of writing a detailed review, but then I had a look at all these 1-star reviews and I honestly laughed my socks off. Almost all of them are brilliant! Better than all the 5-stars reviews actually.<br /><br />On the other hand, I am wondering what people expect to read when they start a story about an oversexed underground fighter and a sweet ex-athlete who doesn't understand what this bad boy wants from her. And moreover when this story is written by a female writer and it is given by the girl's POV. This is romance. And it is fun.<br /><br />And as long as there are girls who watch Roman Reigns and scream "I love you. Take me. I want to have your children!", there will be girls who love Remy aka Remington ‘Riptide’ Tate and his growling.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Why’d you want to have sex with me? To have a fucking adventure? What was I supposed to be? Your one-night-fucking stand? I’m every woman’s adventure, damn you, and I don’t want to be yours. I want to be your fucking REAL. You get that? If I fuck you, I want you to belong to me. To be mine. I want you to give yourself to me—not Riptide!”<br /><br />“I won’t ever be yours if you don’t take me. Take me! You son of a bitch, can’t you see how much I want you?”</i>
</b><br /><br />So yeah, this book made my day...</span>
  <a data-text-id="12309928239210634299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1226231316" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Snow" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31719636-snow"><img alt="Snow" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465808156p2/31719636.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1226231316?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Snow" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Snow" href="/user/show/31719636-snow">Snow</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=alpha">alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=fighters">fighters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=best-ever">best-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1226231316" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16185412099766172670"> <br/><br/> <b>5 *REMINGTON* stars</b><br/><br/><b>Re-read January 8th, 2017</b><br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>And I don’t want the world to see me, it says, but I want you to know who I am…</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/>And yes, <b>Remington "RIPTIDE" Tate aka REMY, is still my absolute No.1 fighter</b> *bows*<br/><br/><b>My first review:</b><br/><br/>I'm quite overwhelmed now...<br/><br/>ok, I slept it over! You know how they say, the morning is better than the evening, in a sense, your thoughts will be clearer in the morning after the hype settles down!<br/><br/>well, guess what? it didn't work for me! <br/><u>who, said that anyway?! P</u></span>
  <span id="freeText16185412099766172670" style="display:none"> <br><br> <b>5 *REMINGTON* stars</b><br><br><b>Re-read January 8th, 2017</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>And I don’t want the world to see me, it says, but I want you to know who I am…</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And yes, <b>Remington "RIPTIDE" Tate aka REMY, is still my absolute No.1 fighter</b> *bows*<br><br><b>My first review:</b><br><br>I'm quite overwhelmed now...<br><br>ok, I slept it over! You know how they say, the morning is better than the evening, in a sense, your thoughts will be clearer in the morning after the hype settles down!<br><br>well, guess what? it didn't work for me! <br><u>who, said that anyway?! Probably a blunt person who didn't have anything to sort out in a first place!!!</u><br><br>ah, hell...lets starts from the end...LOL<br><br>it has a HEA, thank GOD, for that!<br>the book is actually NOT what I expected from a story about the fighter, I mean I knew there would be some issues and problems from the past and all, but this story actually dealt with a serious subject that also draws parallels from real life.<br><br>and that fact pulled me deeper into the story.<br><br>so, we have a fighter (boxer) Remington "Riptide" Tate aka Remy for short<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387482876ra/7604635.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and Brooke Dumas (a former athlete, tracker due to injury turned physical therapist)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426421598i/14013941.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>it was a spark at first sight, an electricity that set the path of their ways and from then on...there was NO stopping for either of them<br><br>he's protective and possesive of her and he's a badass fighter to start with! duh? and he's not thinking twice...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“For the love of fucking god, don’t ever, ever, do that again. EVER. If one of them sets a hand on you, I’ll fucking kill them, and I won’t give a rat’s fuck who watches me!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>the intensity of the story was palpable, the anticipation was a hype, made me frustrated and anxious I was already sreaming inside...<br><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>...I find myself touching his mouth with a lone fingertip. His lips are so plump and firm, but at the same time, smooth and silky. I feel a quick, damp flick as his tongue flashes out to lick me, and a shudder shoots through my spine. He groans and pulls my whole finger into his mouth and closes his eyes as he sucks it.<br>“Remington…” I breathe.<br><br>...he grabs me and plants a kiss on my lips, quick and dry, but it bursts open a wealth of longing inside me he whispers, “You look beautiful.” He runs his thumb with desperation along my jaw, and tilts my chin up, kissing my lips, dry and quick again. “So damn beautiful I couldn’t take my eyes off you all evening.”<br><br>He cups my face in those big hands that make me feel fragile and tiny, and he hungrily recaptures my mouth. He takes it slowly this time, as if I’m precious and valuable. “Tonight you’re mine.”<br><br>His mouth grazes a path down my temple, to my chin, and his lips my buzz, fast and fevered, over mine. “I want you now. I can’t wait to get rid of these people. How do you like it, Brooke? Hard? Fast?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Now I’m screamin’ OMFG, do it already!!!<br><br>I mean, you can't put smth like that to go on for a looooong time, it was killing me, Jesus, will you DO it already, i'm burning up over here...LOL<br><br>I'm ready to explode... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426421598ra/14013942.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>His hands clamp around me, and he crushes me to his body as he slides his nose along the shell of my ear. “When I take you, you’ll be mine,” he says, a soft promise in my ear. He slides his thumb along my jaw, then gently kisses my earlobe. “You need to be certain.” <br><br>“I want you to know me first, and then, I want you to let me know if you still want me to take you.”<br><br>“But I already know I want you,”<br><br>I need you to know who I am. What I am.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>and now I have a big question mark over my head! Like, WTF? What can be so horrible? So devastating? What is holding him back?<br>and I'm not the only one who's asking herself that...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Why won’t you take me, Remington?”<br>He groans and pulls me closer. “Because I want you too much.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>again, please? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426090523ra/13972699.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>let's hear this, again! In case I've missed smth!<br><br>she asks:<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Why haven’t you touched me? Why don’t you fucking take me? Am I too fat? Too plain? Do you just delight in fucking torturing me senseless or are you just plain damn mean? For your information, I’ve wanted to have sexwith you since the day I went into your stupid hotel room and got hired instead!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>And then the handsome SOB throws this to her face:<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Why’d you want to have sex with me? To have a fucking adventure? What was I supposed to be? Your one-night-fucking stand? I’m every woman’s adventure, damn you, and I don’t want to beyours. I want to be your fucking REAL. You get that? If I fuck you, I want you to belong to me. To be mine. I want you to give yourself to me—not Riptide!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Now, that is just absurd! Remy, darlin'?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426421598ra/14013943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then I think there's a catch, right?<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I won’t ever be yours if you don’t take me. Take me! You son of a bitch, can’t you see how much I want you?”<br><br>“You don’t know me,” he strains out through gritted teeth, his face anxious as he clenches my wrists at my sides. “You don’t know the first thing about me.”<br><br>“Then tell me! You think I’ll leave if you tell me whatever it is you don’t want me to know?”<br><br>“I don’t think it, I know it.<br>You’ll leave me the second it gets too steep, and you’ll leave me with nothing—when I want you like I’ve never wanted anything in my life. You’re all I think about, dream about. I get high and low and it’s all about you now, it’s not even about me anymore. I can’t sleep, can’t think, can’t concentrate worth shit anymore and it’s all because I want to be the fucking ‘one’ for you and as soon as you realize what I am, all I’ll be is a fucking mistake!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Remy, you sorry ass, you break my heart, and now not only my carnal parts ache but my heart as well! Well, shit!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>You had me at hello, you fucking asshole! You make me want you until it hurts and then you won’t do shit!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Yeah, I feel you, Brooke! but then he just reveals this...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Because I’m fucking <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[you wish!!! LOL go read the book! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>and YES! It's finally happening...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>He brings his head to mine and pushes his tongue until I swallow my own gasps. “You wanted me.” His breaths come fast, his eyes wild. “Here I am.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>the story continues to grow after bursting, they both have so much to learn, to deal with, in an out, and YES, f*cking pride being the big asshole, right there...in their way<br><br>this was a beautifuly written story about <b>emotions</b> above all, dealing and recognizing them...and then acting upon them...woven real life problems just bring the dose of reality that is unescapable...but then you don't even wanna do that...cause you're already hooked!<br><br>they make mistakes, shit, they'll probably continue to do them as well, a lot of them, hell, you can make a shopping list but they acknowledge them all and they are coping...and that's the first step!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I love you. I love you.” His breath seizes in his chest, and I continue in a rush. “More than I’ve ever thought it possible to love any other human being. <br><br>...it tears me open to ask you to be with me when I know I’m just going to do something to fucking hurt you again!”<br><br>“Yes! Yes you probably are, you idiot! And it’s going to be a damned skydive for me, and I’m going to hang on tight and just jump with you because that’s what you do to me. <br><br> ...I’m crazy about you...<br> ...it’s you I want... <br> ...it’s always been about you... <br> ...i want to be with you... <br><br>I want you to love me back, Remy. You’ve never told me how you feel about me!”<br><br>“I’m yours now, and you can’t ditch me like you just did. Even if I screw this up, I’ll still be your screw-up.”<br><br>“Not my screw-up. My real.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I couldn't present this review any differently! There were so many things i wanted to say myself, and then I practicaly USED every possible line from the book, and if that isn't one huge spoiler, i don't know what is! LOL<br><br>#sorryNOTsorry<br><br>but I'm too lost in it, now!<br> And there's no going back!<br><br><b>Loved it, cause it was fuckin REAL</b> (but not burdening...)<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer589378720" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13058013294716153898">Meet Remington 'Riptide' Tate & Brooke Dumas<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417492i/825845._SX540_.jpg' width='380' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><br/>Remy is a fighter and he is all alpha!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417492i/825846._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brooke is a sports rehab specialist and a former Olympic contender.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417492i/825847._SX540_.jpg' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are so many "lion" references and mannerisms throughout the book that I couldn't resist using the pictures above.<br/><br/><b>SERIES:</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17617277.Real__Real___1_' title='Real (Real, #1) by Katy Evans' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363442697s/17617277.jpg' alt='Real (Real, #1) by Katy Evans' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17792606.Mine__Real___2_' title='Mine (Real, #2) by Katy Evans' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1377178049s/17792606.jpg' alt='Mine (Real, #2) by Katy Evans' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17830559.Remy__Real___3_' title='Remy (Real, #3) by Katy Evans' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1379702539s/17830559.jpg' alt='Remy (Real, #3) by Katy Evans' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17830561.Rogue__Real___4_' title='Rogue (Real, #4) by Katy Evans' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394716297s/17830561.jpg' alt='Rogue (Real, #4) by Katy Evans' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17830562.Ripped__Real___5_' title='Ripped (Real, #5) by Katy Evans' rel='nofollow noopener'>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bM6SRxn0njFwjBg3MK3Np9fK1L9W94lODv1sbivP91FW6PuVoqpXWdenrFbHWMd4AZUzd5h6BylVgyrf5owFyw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xZyJbXqcOeB5SbVnLL3l64g2yexdQHY1jQ5bq8kPKAv/uuC/wcLwiN5iAQbbSO80XmkuJJPN+FLWcB0aBEzakQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

//<![CDATA[
      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_16140036'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140036-this-man?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">This Man (This Man, #1)<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/6576110.Jodi_Ellen_Malpas?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Jodi Ellen Malpas<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.10 avg rating &mdash; 99,948 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2012\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer18246733198902446842\">Young interior designer Ava O’Shea has an appointment for a first consultation at The Manor with the owner, Mr Jesse Ward. She is expecting nothing more than an overweight, cravat wearing, well-to-do countryman, and on arrival, nothing would suggest <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText18246733198902446842\" style=\"display:none\">Young interior designer Ava O’Shea has an appointment for a first consultation at The Manor with the owner, Mr Jesse Ward. She is expecting nothing more than an overweight, cravat wearing, well-to-do countryman, and on arrival, nothing would suggest otherwise. How wrong could she be? This Man is devastatingly handsome, charming and confident. He is also a conceited, hedonistic playboy, who knows no boundaries.
